          , t = n.split("");

            var f = n.indexOf(r), e, o;
            if (f > -1) {
                for (n = n.split(""),
                t[f] = "(" + i.regex + ")",
                n[f] = "$",

                    index: f,
                    apply: i.apply
                })
            }
        }),

            regex: new RegExp("^" + t.join("") + "$"),
            map: i(u, "index")
        }
    }
    function f(n, t, i) {

            }

            }

                this.month = n - 1
            }
        },

            }

            }

            }

            }

            }

    }

    }

    };

                top: 0,
                left: 0
            }, i = u(t[0]), f;

                top: r.top + (t.pageYOffset || n[0].documentElement.scrollTop),
                left: r.left + (t.pageXOffset || n[0].documentElement.scrollLeft)
            }
        },
        positionElements: function(n, t, i, r) {

            u = r ? this.offset(n) : this.position(n);
            h = t.prop("offsetWidth");
            c = t.prop("offsetHeight");
            o = {
                center: function() {
                    return u.left + u.width / 2 - h / 2
                },
                left: function() {
                    return u.left
                },
                right: function() {
                    return u.left + u.width
                }
            };
            s = {
                center: function() {
                    return u.top + u.height / 2 - c / 2
                },
                top: function() {
                    return u.top
                },
                bottom: function() {
                    return u.top + u.height
                }
            };
            switch (l) {
            case "right":
                f = {
                    top: s[e](),
                    left: o[l]()
                };
                break;
            case "left":
                f = {
                    top: s[e](),
                    left: u.left - h
                };
                break;
            case "bottom":
                f = {
                    top: s[l](),
                    left: o[e]()
                };
                break;
            default:
                f = {
                    top: u.top - c,
                    left: o[e]()
                }
            }
            return f
        }
    }
}

    return {
        createNew: function() {
            var n = [];
            return {
                add: function(t, i) {
                    n.push({
                        key: t,
                        value: i
                    })
                },
                get: function(t) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < n.length; i++)
                        if (t == n[i].key)
                            return n[i]
                },
                keys: function() {
                    for (var i = [], t = 0; t < n.length; t++)
                        i.push(n[t].key);
                    return i
                },
                top: function() {
                    return n[n.length - 1]

                            r = i;
                            break

                },

                },
                length: function() {
                    return n.length
                }
            }
        }
    }

    }

    }
    ;
    n.noNext = function() {
        return n.page === n.totalPages
    }

}).controller("TimepickerController", ["$scope", "$attrs", "$parse", "$log", "$locale", "timepickerConfig", function(n, t, i, r, u, f) {
    function w() {
        var t = parseInt(n.hours, 10)
          , i = n.showMeridian ? t > 0 && 13 > t : t >= 0 && 24 > t;
        if (i)
            return (n.showMeridian && (12 === t && (t = 0),
            n.meridian === d[1] && (t += 12)),
            t)
    }
    function b() {
        var t = parseInt(n.minutes, 10);
        if (t >= 0 && 60 > t)
            return t
    }
    function y(n) {
        return angular.isDefined(n) && n.toString().length < 2 ? "0" + n : n.toString()
    }
    function p(n) {
        g();
        o.$setViewValue(new Date(e));
        k(n)
